def get_pipeline(sector_filter: str = "", stage_filter: str = "", limit: int = 500) -> dict:
    global _pipeline_cache
    if _pipeline_cache is None:

        _saved_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")

        try:
            for name, prof in _CP.items():
                try:
                    raw_src = prof.get("profile_source", "")
                    if raw_src != "verified":
                        continue
                    result = score(prof)
                    bm = result.get("bundle_match") or {}
                    ps = result.get("premium_summary") or {}
                    sc = result.get("scores") or {}
                    top_risks = result.get("top_risks") or []
                    scores_vals = [v for v in sc.values() if isinstance(v, (int, float))]
                    avg_score = round(sum(scores_vals) / len(scores_vals), 1) if scores_vals else 0
                    src = "verified"
                    stage = prof.get("funding_stage", "")
                    if stage == "Pre-seed":
                        tap = "preseed"
                    elif stage == "Seed":
                        tap = "untapped"
                    elif stage == "Series A":
                        tap = "strike_now"
                    else:
                        tap = "covered"
                    sector = prof.get("sector", "")
                    inc = _incumbent(stage, sector)
                    max_l = ps.get("max_lakh", 0)
                    _stage_yr = {"Pre-seed": 1, "Seed": 2, "Series A": 4, "Series B+": 7}
                    rows.append({
                        "startup_name": name,
                        "sector": sector,
                        "funding_stage": stage,
                        "bundle_name": bm.get("name", ""),
                        "min_lakh": ps.

Bash Read _balanced_pipeline_rows source

python -c "
import sys, inspect
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
import os; os.chdir(r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web')
import server
print(inspect.getsource(server._balanced_pipeline_rows))
" 2>&1

OUT
[startup] .env loaded — GEMINI_API_KEY SET
def _balanced_pipeline_rows(rows: list[dict], limit: int) -> list[dict]:
    """Keep the default opportunity list stage-balanced instead of Series B+ dominated."""
    if limit <= 0:
        return []

    stage_order = ["Pre-seed", "Seed", "Series A", "Series B+"]
    buckets = {stage: [r for r in rows if r.get("funding_stage") == stage] for stage in stage_order}
    other_rows = [r for r in rows if r.get("funding_stage") not in buckets]

    balanced = []
    for stage in stage_order:
        balanced.extend(buckets[stage])
    balanced.extend(other_rows)
    return balanced[:limit]

def get_pipeline(sector_filter: str = "", stage_filter: str = "", limit: int = 500) -> dict:
    global _pipeline_cache
    if _pipeline_cache is None:
        from company_profiles import COMPANY_PROFILES as _CP
        rows = []
        _saved_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
        os.environ["GEMINI_API_KEY"] = ""  # force deterministic — no Gemini during pipeline scoring
        try:
            for name, prof in _CP.items():
                try:
                    raw_src = prof.get("profile_source", "")
                    if raw_src != "verified":
                        continue
                    result = score(prof)
                    bm = result.get("bundle_match") or {}
                    ps = result.get("premium_summary") or {}
                    sc = result.get("scores") or {}
                    top_risks = result.get("top_risks") or []
                    scores_vals = [v for v in sc.values() if isinstance(v, (int, float))]
                    avg_score = round(sum(scores_vals) / len(scores_vals), 1) if scores_vals else 0
                    src = "verified"
                    stage = prof.get("funding_stage", "")
                    if stage == "Pre-seed":
                        tap = "preseed"
                    elif stage == "Seed":
                        tap = "untapped"
                    elif stage == "Series A":
                        tap = "strike_now"
                    else:
                        tap = "covered"
                    sector = prof.get("sector", "")
                    inc = _incumbent(stage, sector)
                    max_l = ps.get("max_lakh", 0)
                    _stage_yr = {"Pre-seed": 1, "Seed": 2, "Series A": 4, "Series B+": 7}
                    rows.append({
                        "startup_name": name,
                        "sector": sector,
                        "funding_stage": stage,
                        "bundle_name": bm.get("name", ""),
                        "min_lakh": ps.get("min_lakh", 0),
                        "max_lakh": max_l,
                        "overall_score": avg_score,
                        "top_risk": top_risks[0].get("name", "") if top_risks else "",
                        "profile_source": src,
                        "tap_status": tap,
                        # enriched fields
                        "city": (prof.get("state_footprint") or ["India"])[0],
                        "founded": max(2012, 2024 - _stage_yr.get(stage, 3)),
                        "team": prof.get("team_size", 0),
                        "revenue": prof.get("annual_revenue_cr", 0),
                        "operations": ", ".join((prof.get("physical_assets") or [])[:2]) or "Digital-first",
                        "incumbent": inc,
                        "signal": _signal(tap, name),
                        "opp": 0,
                        "bundle_lines": _bundle_lines(bm, max_l),
                        "pitch": _pitch_angle(sector, inc),
                        "drivers": [tr.get("name", "") for tr in (top_risks or [])[:3]],
                    })
                except Exception as _exc:
                    print(f"[pipeline] skip '{name}': {_exc}", flush=True)
        finally:
            if _saved_key:
                os.environ["GEMINI_API_KEY"] = _saved_key
            else:
                os.environ.pop("GEMINI_API_KEY", None)
        for row in rows:
            row["opp"] = _opp_score(row)
        stage_rank = {"Pre-seed": 0, "Seed": 1, "Series A": 2, "Series B+": 3}
        rows.sort(key=lambda r: (stage_rank.get(r["funding_stage"], 9), -r["max_lakh"], r["startup_name"].lower()))
        _pipeline_cache = rows

    filtered = _pipeline_cache
    if sector_filter:
        sf = sector_filter.lower()
        filtered = [r for r in filtered if sf in r["sector"].lower()]
    if stage_filter:
        stf = stage_filter.lower()
        filtered = [r for r in filtered if r["funding_stage"].lower() == stf]

    displayed = filtered[:limit] if stage_filter else _balanced_pipeline_rows(filtered, limit)

    total_pool_cr = round(sum(r["max_lakh"] for r in displayed) / 100, 1)
    untapped = [r for r in displayed if r["tap_status"] in ("untapped", "strike_now")]
    untapped_pool_cr = round(sum(r["max_lakh"] for r in untapped) / 100, 1)
    sectors = [r["sector"] for r in displayed if r["sector"]]
    top_sector = max(set(sectors), key=sectors.count) if sectors else ""
    avg_score = round(sum(r["overall_score"] for r in displayed) / len(displayed), 1) if displayed else 0

    return {
        "companies": displayed,
        "total": len(displayed),
        "kpis": {
            "total_companies": len(displayed),
            "total_pool_cr": total_pool_cr,
            "untapped_pool_cr": untapped_pool_cr,
            "untapped_count": len(untapped),
            "top_sector": top_sector,
            "avg_risk_score": avg_score,
        },
    }
I see the issue. When no stage filter is applied, get_pipeline calls _balanced_pipeline_rows(filtered, limit) with limit=500. But the default API call from renderPipelineDashboard in app.js probably calls with a lower limit. Let me check what limit app.js passes to /api/pipeline.

Actually wait - _balanced_pipeline_rows now just returns balanced[:limit] where limit=500, so if there are 263 companies it should return all 263. But the user says only 197 are showing.

Let me check what the actual API call from renderPipelineDashboard looks like. What URL/params does it use?

The real problem is that the server's _pipeline_cache is stale—it was built before the company_profiles enrichment added those extra companies. Since the server only processes profiles with profile_source == "verified" and the verified_companies.json file was modified, the cache needs to be refreshed by restarting the server. The user is seeing 197 companies because that's what was cached before the enrichment happened.

Now let me check how many verified companies actually exist and what limit the frontend is requesting:

1221:       const res = await fetch("/api/pipeline?limit=500");
The frontend requests /api/pipeline?limit=500 and there are 263 verified companies. So with limit=500, _balanced_pipeline_rows(filtered, 500) should return all 263. The issue must be a stale _pipeline_cache in the running server.

The server's _pipeline_cache was built when there were fewer verified companies (197 or 194). Since it's a module-level singleton, it won't rebuild until the server is restarted.

The user needs to restart their server. That's the only fix here. The code is correct, the data is correct (263 verified), but the running server has cached an old result.

So I'll recommend restarting the server to clear the stale cache and resolve this.

The code and data are both fine — 263 verified companies exist, frontend requests 500, _balanced_pipeline_rows doesn't cap anything. The problem is the running server has a stale in-memory cache built before the companies were enriched.

Just restart your server. Kill it and run python server.py again — the cache rebuilds on first request and you'll see all 263.

So the fix is: the user needs to do a hard browser refresh (Ctrl+F5 or Ctrl+Shift+R) to clear the JavaScript _pipelineData cache and force a fresh fetch from the server.

import sys, ast, re
sys.stdout.reconfigure(encoding='utf-8')
from company_profiles import COMPANY_PROFILES as CP

to_remove = {name for name, prof in CP.items() if (prof.get('annual_revenue_cr') or 0) > 100}
print(f'Removing {len(to_remove)} companies')

path = 'company_profiles.py'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

removed = 0
for name in to_remove:
    # Match the entry: \"Name\": { ... }, including trailing comma/newline
    # Use a regex that matches from the quoted key to the closing brace+comma
    pattern = r'[ \t]+' + re.escape(json_key(name)) + r'\s*:\s*\{[^{}]*(?:\{[^{}]*\}[^{}]*)*\},?\n'
    import json
    key = json.dumps(name)
    pattern = r'[ \t]*' + re.escape(key) + r'\s*:\s*\{[^}]*(?:\{[^}]*\}[^}]*)*\},?\n'
    matches = re.findall(pattern, content)
    if matches:
        removed += 1
print(f'Found via regex: {removed}')

Bash Add email field after startup name in the identity section
IN
python -c "
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\app.js'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = '''      <div class=\"field-group\">
        <label>Startup name</label>
        <input class=\"f-input\" id=\"f-name\" type=\"text\" placeholder=\"e.g. Acme Labs\" value=\"\${esc(p.startup_name||\"\")}\" oninput=\"setVal('startup_name',this.value)\" />
      </div>'''

new = '''      <div class=\"field-group\">
        <label>Startup name</label>
        <input class=\"f-input\" id=\"f-name\" type=\"text\" placeholder=\"e.g. Acme Labs\" value=\"\${esc(p.startup_name||\"\")}\" oninput=\"setVal('startup_name',this.value)\" />
      </div>

      <div class=\"field-group\">
        <label>Founder / contact email</label>
        <input class=\"f-input\" id=\"f-email\" type=\"email\" placeholder=\"e.g. founder@acmelabs.com\" value=\"\${esc(p.contact_email||\"\")}\" oninput=\"setVal('contact_email',this.value)\" />
      </div>'''

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print('PATCHED')
else:
    print('NOT FOUND')
"

Bash Add contact_email to autofill prompt and persist record
IN
python -c "
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\server.py'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# 1. Add contact_email to the prompt
old_prompt = '  \"payment_or_card_program\": <true or false>\n}}\n\nReturn ONLY the JSON object. No explanation, no markdown fences.\"\"\"'
new_prompt = '  \"payment_or_card_program\": <true or false>,\n  \"contact_email\": <founder or primary contact email address if publicly available, else null>\n}}\n\nReturn ONLY the JSON object. No explanation, no markdown fences.\"\"\"'

# 2. Add contact_email to _persist_verified_profile record
old_record = '            \"profile_source\": \"verified\",\n        }'
new_record = '            \"contact_email\": profile.get(\"contact_email\", \"\"),\n            \"profile_source\": \"verified\",\n        }'

c1 = content.replace(old_prompt, new_prompt)
c2 = c1.replace(old_record, new_record)

changed = (c1 != content) + (c2 != c1)
with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(c2)
print(f'Patches applied: {changed}/2')
"

Bash Add nav history globals and functions
IN
python -c "
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\app.js'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# 1. Add nav history globals after state declaration
old_globals = '''/* ─── UTILS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */'''
new_globals = '''/* ─── NAVIGATION HISTORY ────────────────────────────────────── */
let _navHistory = [];   // [{label, fn, args}]
let _navPos     = -1;   // current position in history

function _navLabel(view) {
  return { role: 'Home', signals: 'Signal Radar', pipeline: 'Pipeline', customer: 'Customer Quote', underwriter: 'Risk Form', results: 'Results', loading: null }[view] || view;
}

function navPush(fn, ...args) {
  // Truncate forward history when branching
  _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1);
  _navHistory.push({ fn, args, view: state.view });
  _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1;
  fn(...args);
  _updateNavButtons();
}

function navBack() {
  if (_navPos <= 0) return;
  _navPos--;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _updateNavButtons();
}

function navForward() {
  if (_navPos >= _navHistory.length - 1) return;
  _navPos++;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _updateNavButtons();
}

function _updateNavButtons() {
  const bar = document.getElementById('nav-history-bar');
  if (!bar) return;
  const backBtn = document.getElementById('nav-back-btn');
  const fwdBtn  = document.getElementById('nav-fwd-btn');
  const label   = document.getElementById('nav-crumb');
  if (backBtn) backBtn.disabled = _navPos <= 0;
  if (fwdBtn)  fwdBtn.disabled  = _navPos >= _navHistory.length - 1;
  if (label) {
    const prev = _navPos > 0 ? _navHistory[_navPos - 1] : null;
    const next = _navPos < _navHistory.length - 1 ? _navHistory[_navPos + 1] : null;
    backBtn && (backBtn.title = prev ? 'Back to ' + _navLabel(prev.view) : 'No history');
    fwdBtn  && (fwdBtn.title  = next ? 'Forward to ' + _navLabel(next.view) : 'Nothing ahead');
  }
  bar.style.display = _navHistory.length > 1 ? 'flex' : 'none';
}

function _injectNavBar() {
  if (document.getElementById('nav-history-bar')) return;
  const bar = document.createElement('div');
  bar.id = 'nav-history-bar';
  bar.innerHTML = \`
    <button id=\"nav-back-btn\" class=\"nav-hist-btn\" onclick=\"navBack()\" disabled title=\"Back\">&#8592;</button>
    <button id=\"nav-fwd-btn\"  class=\"nav-hist-btn\" onclick=\"navForward()\" disabled title=\"Forward\">&#8594;</button>
  \`;
  document.body.appendChild(bar);
  _updateNavButtons();
}

/* ─── UTILS ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */'''

if old_globals in content:
    content = content.replace(old_globals, new_globals)
    print('Step 1: nav globals OK')
else:
    print('Step 1: FAILED')

with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(content)
" 2>&1

OUT
Step 1: nav globals OK

Bash Inject history push into all top-level render functions
IN
python -c "
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\app.js'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

# Add _navCalledByHistory flag and modify each render function to push to history
# Strategy: Add a flag, set it when nav back/forward is called, check it in renders

# First replace the navBack/navForward to set a flag
old_navback = '''function navBack() {
  if (_navPos <= 0) return;
  _navPos--;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _updateNavButtons();
}

function navForward() {
  if (_navPos >= _navHistory.length - 1) return;
  _navPos++;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _updateNavButtons();
}'''

new_navback = '''let _navCalledByHistory = false;

function navBack() {
  if (_navPos <= 0) return;
  _navPos--;
  _navCalledByHistory = true;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _navCalledByHistory = false;
  _updateNavButtons();
}

function navForward() {
  if (_navPos >= _navHistory.length - 1) return;
  _navPos++;
  _navCalledByHistory = true;
  const entry = _navHistory[_navPos];
  entry.fn(...entry.args);
  _navCalledByHistory = false;
  _updateNavButtons();
}'''

content = content.replace(old_navback, new_navback)

# Now add _navPush helper inside each top-level render function
# renderRoleSelection
content = content.replace(
    'function renderRoleSelection() {\n  state.view = \"role\";',
    'function renderRoleSelection() {\n  state.view = \"role\";\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderRoleSelection, args: [], view: \"role\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

# renderSignalRadarDashboard
content = content.replace(
    'async function renderSignalRadarDashboard(filter = _signalRadarFilter, forceRefresh = false) {\n  state.view = \"signals\";',
    'async function renderSignalRadarDashboard(filter = _signalRadarFilter, forceRefresh = false) {\n  state.view = \"signals\";\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderSignalRadarDashboard, args: [filter, false], view: \"signals\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

# renderPipelineDashboard
content = content.replace(
    'async function renderPipelineDashboard(sectorFilter = \"\", stageFilter = \"\", tapFilter = \"untapped\") {\n  state.view = \"pipeline\";',
    'async function renderPipelineDashboard(sectorFilter = \"\", stageFilter = \"\", tapFilter = \"untapped\") {\n  state.view = \"pipeline\";\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderPipelineDashboard, args: [sectorFilter, stageFilter, tapFilter], view: \"pipeline\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

# renderCustomerInput
content = content.replace(
    'function renderCustomerInput() {\n  state.view = \"customer\";',
    'function renderCustomerInput() {\n  state.view = \"customer\";\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderCustomerInput, args: [], view: \"customer\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

# renderForm (underwriter)
content = content.replace(
    'function renderForm() {\n  state.view = \"underwriter\";',
    'function renderForm() {\n  state.view = \"underwriter\";\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderForm, args: [], view: \"underwriter\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

# renderResults — push with a closure that re-renders the last result
content = content.replace(
    'function renderResults(result) {\n  result = normalizeGroupSafeguardCompanion(result);',
    'function renderResults(result) {\n  result = normalizeGroupSafeguardCompanion(result);\n  if (!_navCalledByHistory) { const _r = result; _navHistory = _navHistory.slice(0, _navPos + 1); _navHistory.push({ fn: renderResults, args: [_r], view: \"results\" }); _navPos = _navHistory.length - 1; setTimeout(_updateNavButtons, 0); }'
)

with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(content)

The "Mandate Card" — An exclusive membership card style with embossed gold or white text on a dark background, premium as the key identifier, and covers as classified line items.

The "War Room Brief" — Each bundle cover presented as a briefing item.

Now I'm building the Coverage Stack interface where each cover gets its own card that fans out with CSS transforms, expands on interaction to reveal the "why" text, and displays the premium below the entire stack. I need to design the CSS and JavaScript to handle the stacking effect and expand/collapse behavior.

For the visual layout, I'm positioning cards absolutely within a relative container, rotating and offsetting each one to create that fanned appearance with an entrance animation. The challenge with 5+ covers is that a pure fan gets crowded, so I'm thinking a card deck approach where you can browse through them feels cleaner than trying to fan everything at once.

The most compelling option is a "deal" animation where cards spread out from a stack like a poker hand, each displaying the cover icon, name, a brief explanation, and a mandatory/optional indicator. On hover, cards flip or expand to reveal the full details. For larger collections, I'll use a horizontal carousel with slight overlap so users can scroll through and interact with each card.

Bash Replace renderBundleHero with card stack version
IN
python -c "
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\app.js'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

start = content.find('function renderBundleHero(bundle, recs, why = {})')
end   = content.find('\nfunction renderBundleAlternatives', start)
old_fn = content[start:end]

new_fn = r'''function renderBundleHero(bundle, recs, why = {}) {
  if (!bundle?.name) return \`<div class=\"r-card\">\${emptyState(\"📦\", \"No bundle matched\", \"No packaged bundle was a strong enough fit for this profile. Recommended products are listed individually below.\")}</div>\`;

  const mandatory = bundle.mandatory_covers || [];
  const optional  = bundle.optional_covers  || [];
  const companion = bundle.companion_bundle  || null;
  const eyebrow   = bundle.nearest_fallback ? "Closest package fit" : "Recommended package";
  const isOfficial = bundle.is_real_il_bundle === true || OFFICIAL_IL_BUNDLE_NAMES.has(bundle.name);

  const allCovers = [
    ...mandatory.map(c => ({ key: c, type: "mandatory" })),
    ...optional.map(c  => ({ key: c, type: "optional"  })),
  ];
  const companionCovers = companion ? [
    ...(companion.mandatory_covers || []).map(c => ({ key: c, type: "mandatory" })),
    ...(companion.optional_covers  || []).map(c => ({ key: c, type: "optional"  })),
  ] : [];

  // Two-letter abbreviations for the card glyph
  const GLYPHS = {
    PI_TECH_EO: "PI", D_AND_O: "DO", CYBER: "CY", CRIME_FIDELITY: "CF",
    EMPLOYMENT_PRACTICES: "EP", CGL: "GL", PROPERTY: "PR", MARINE_CARGO: "MC",
    WORKMEN_COMP: "WC", PRODUCT_LIABILITY: "PL", STATUTORY_LIABILITY: "SL",
    BUSINESS_INTERRUPTION: "BI", FIDELITY: "FI", KEY_MAN: "KM",
    DIRECTORS_LIABILITY: "DO", PROFESSIONAL_INDEMNITY: "PI",
  };
  const glyph = key => GLYPHS[key] || key.slice(0, 2).toUpperCase();

  const n = allCovers.length;
  const maxRot = Math.min(3.5 * n, 22); // total half-spread in degrees

  const cards = allCovers.map(({ key, type }, i) => {
    const label = labelize(key);
    const blurb = getCoverWhy(key, why, "bundle_covers") || "";
    // Fan: evenly distribute rotations from -maxRot to +maxRot
    const rot = n > 1 ? -maxRot + (i / (n - 1)) * maxRot * 2 : 0;
    const yOff = (Math.abs(rot) * 1.8).toFixed(1);
    return \`
      <div class="cstack-card \${type}" style="--rot:\${rot.toFixed(1)}deg;--yoff:\${yOff}px;--i:\${i}" tabindex="0" aria-label="\${esc(label)}">
        <div class="cstack-inner">
          <span class="cstack-badge \${type}">\${type === "mandatory" ? "Mandatory" : "Optional"}</span>
          <div class="cstack-glyph">\${glyph(key)}</div>
          <div class="cstack-name">\${esc(label)}</div>
          <div class="cstack-blurb">\${esc(blurb)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>\`;
  }).join("");

  const companionSection = companion?.name ? \`
    <div class="cstack-companion">
      <span class="cstack-companion-kicker">+ Companion: \${esc(companion.name)}</span>
      <div class="cstack-companion-pills">
        \${companionCovers.map(({ key, type }) => \`<span class="cstack-cpill \${type}">\${esc(labelize(key))}</span>\`).join("")}
      </div>
    </div>\` : "";

  return \`
    <div class="bundle-stack-wrap">

      <div class="bundle-stack-header">
        <div class="bundle-stack-left">
          <div class="bundle-stack-eyebrow">\${eyebrow}</div>
          <div class="bundle-stack-name">\${esc(bundle.name)}</div>
          \${bundle.il_product_name ? \`<div class="bundle-stack-il">\${esc(bundle.il_product_name)}</div>\` : ""}
          \${bundle.description ? \`<div class="bundle-stack-desc">\${esc(bundle.description)}</div>\` : ""}
          \${why?.bundle ? \`<div class="bundle-why-note">\${esc(why.bundle)}</div>\` : ""}
        </div>
        <div class="bundle-stack-right">
          <div class="bundle-fit-badge"><div class="bundle-fit-dot"></div>\${bundle.fit_pct || 0}% fit</div>
          <span class="bstack-official \${isOfficial ? "real" : "curated"}">\${isOfficial ? "Official IL Product" : "Curated Cover Set"}</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="cstack-deck-label">\${mandatory.length} mandatory · \${optional.length} optional · hover any card to read</div>

      <div class="cstack-deck" style="--n:\${n}">
        \${cards}
      </div>

      \${companionSection}

      \${(bundle.prerequisite_notes || []).map(note => \`<div class="bundle-prereq-note">\${esc(note)}</div>\`).join("")}
    </div>\`;
}
'''

content = content[:start] + new_fn + content[end:]
with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    f.write(content)
print('renderBundleHero replaced')

new_fn = """function renderBundleHero(bundle, recs, why = {}) {
  if (!bundle?.name) return `<div class="r-card">${emptyState("📦", "No bundle matched", "No packaged bundle was a strong enough fit for this profile. Recommended products are listed individually below.")}</div>`;

  const mandatory = bundle.mandatory_covers || [];
  const optional  = bundle.optional_covers  || [];
  const companion = bundle.companion_bundle  || null;
  const eyebrow   = bundle.nearest_fallback ? "Closest package fit" : "Recommended package";
  const isOfficial = bundle.is_real_il_bundle === true || OFFICIAL_IL_BUNDLE_NAMES.has(bundle.name);

  const allCovers = [
    ...mandatory.map(c => ({ key: c, type: "mandatory" })),
    ...optional.map(c  => ({ key: c, type: "optional"  })),
  ];
  const companionCovers = companion ? [
    ...(companion.mandatory_covers || []).map(c => ({ key: c, type: "mandatory" })),
    ...(companion.optional_covers  || []).map(c => ({ key: c, type: "optional"  })),
  ] : [];

  const GLYPHS = {
    PI_TECH_EO: "PI", D_AND_O: "DO", CYBER: "CY", CRIME_FIDELITY: "CF",
    EMPLOYMENT_PRACTICES: "EP", CGL: "GL", PROPERTY: "PR", MARINE_CARGO: "MC",
    WORKMEN_COMP: "WC", PRODUCT_LIABILITY: "PL", STATUTORY_LIABILITY: "SL",
    BUSINESS_INTERRUPTION: "BI", FIDELITY: "FI", KEY_MAN: "KM",
  };
  const glyph = key => (GLYPHS[key] || key.slice(0, 2)).toUpperCase();

  const n = allCovers.length;
  const maxRot = Math.min(3.5 * n, 22);

  const cards = allCovers.map(({ key, type }, i) => {
    const label = labelize(key);
    const blurb = getCoverWhy(key, why, "bundle_covers") || "";
    const rot = n > 1 ? (-maxRot + (i / (n - 1)) * maxRot * 2).toFixed(1) : 0;
    const yOff = (Math.abs(Number(rot)) * 1.8).toFixed(1);
    return `
      <div class="cstack-card ${type}" style="--rot:${rot}deg;--yoff:${yOff}px;--i:${i}" tabindex="0" aria-label="${esc(label)}">
        <div class="cstack-inner">
          <span class="cstack-badge ${type}">${type === "mandatory" ? "Mandatory" : "Optional"}</span>
          <div class="cstack-glyph">${glyph(key)}</div>
          <div class="cstack-name">${esc(label)}</div>
          <div class="cstack-blurb">${esc(blurb)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }).join("");

  const companionSection = companion?.name ? `
    <div class="cstack-companion">
      <span class="cstack-companion-kicker">+ Companion: ${esc(companion.name)}</span>
      <div class="cstack-companion-pills">
        ${companionCovers.map(({ key, type }) => `<span class="cstack-cpill ${type}">${esc(labelize(key))}</span>`).join("")}
      </div>
    </div>` : "";

  return `
    <div class="bundle-stack-wrap">
      <div class="bundle-stack-header">
        <div class="bundle-stack-left">
          <div class="bundle-stack-eyebrow">${eyebrow}</div>
          <div class="bundle-stack-name">${esc(bundle.name)}</div>
          ${bundle.il_product_name ? `<div class="bundle-stack-il">${esc(bundle.il_product_name)}</div>` : ""}
          ${bundle.description ? `<div class="bundle-stack-desc">${esc(bundle.description)}</div>` : ""}
          ${why?.bundle ? `<div class="bundle-why-note">${esc(why.bundle)}</div>` : ""}
        </div>
        <div class="bundle-stack-right">
          <div class="bundle-fit-badge"><div class="bundle-fit-dot"></div>${bundle.fit_pct || 0}% fit</div>
          <span class="bstack-official ${isOfficial ? "real" : "curated"}">${isOfficial ? "Official IL Product" : "Curated Cover Set"}</span>
        </div>

      ${companionSection}

      ${(bundle.prerequisite_notes || []).map(note => `<div class="bundle-prereq-note">${esc(note)}</div>`).join("")}

def get_signal_radar(limit: int = 30, live: bool = True) -> dict:
    profiles = _verified_profiles()
    source_status = "fallback"
    source_error = ""
    articles = []
    seen_article_keys = set()

    def add_articles(new_articles: list[dict]) -> int:
        added = 0
        for article in new_articles:
            key = (article.get("url") or article.get("title") or "").strip().lower()
            if not key or key in seen_article_keys:
                continue
            seen_article_keys.add(key)
            articles.append(article)
            added += 1
            if len(articles) >= max(limit, 12):
                break
        return added

    if live:
        live_sources = []
        try:
            if add_articles(_fetch_direct_rss_signal_articles(limit=max(limit, 12))):
                live_sources.append("rss")
        except Exception as exc:
            source_error = type(exc).__name__
        try:
            if add_articles(_fetch_google_news_signal_articles(limit=max(limit, 12))):
                live_sources.append("google_news")
        except Exception as exc:
            source_error = source_error or type(exc).__name__
        if live_sources:
            source_status = "live_multi" if len(live_sources) > 1 else f"live_{live_sources[0]}"
        if not articles:
            try:
                if add_articles(_fetch_gdelt_signal_articles(limit=max(limit, 12))):
                    source_status = "live_gdelt"
                source_error = "" if articles else source_error
            except Exception as exc:
                source_error = source_error or type(exc).__name__
    if not articles:
        articles = FALLBACK_SIGNAL_ARTICLES

    seen = set()
    tasks = []
    _saved_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    os.environ["GEMINI_API_KEY"] = ""
    try:
        for article in articles:
            task = _signal_task_from_article(article, profiles)
            if not task:
                continue
            key = (task["company"].lower(), task["signal_id"])
            if key in seen:
                continue
            seen.add(key)
            tasks.append(task)
            if len(tasks) >= limit:
                break
    finally:
        if _saved_key:
            os.environ["GEMINI_API_KEY"] = _saved_key
        else:
            os.environ.pop("GEMINI_API_KEY", None)

    high_conf = [t for t in tasks if t.get("confidence", 0) >= 70]
    premium_pool = round(sum(float(t.get("premium_max_lakh") or 0) for t in tasks) / 100, 1)
    signal_counts = {}
    for task in tasks:
        signal_counts[task["signal"]] = signal_counts.get(task["signal"], 0) + 1
    top_signal = max(signal_counts, key=signal_counts.get) if signal_counts else ""

    return {
        "signals": tasks,
        "kpis": {
            "total": len(tasks),
            "high_confidence": len(high_conf),
            "premium_pool_cr": premium_pool,
            "top_signal": top_signal,
        },
        "source_status": s
Yes, it's legit. Here's what's actually happening:

The Signal Radar is real, not a mockup. When you open it, the server:

Fetches live articles from three real sources in priority order — RSS feeds, Google News, and GDELT (a global news database). Falls back to a hardcoded set only if all three fail.

Matches articles to your verified company database — it looks for mentions of companies you already have profiles for, so signals are only shown for startups in your pipeline.

Classifies each signal (funding round, warehouse, IPO, etc.), assigns a confidence score, and maps it to the relevant insurance products — exactly like the table on the home screen.

Returns RM-ready tasks — each signal becomes an actionable item: company, trigger, recommended bundle, confidence %, premium estimate.

The table on the home screen is just documentation of the mapping logic — it's accurate. Funding round → D&O/Key Person/Cyber is correct insurance reasoning. All seven mappings are solid.

The one honest caveat: it says "proposed lead engine" because the signal detection quality depends entirely on whether the news sources mention your specific verified companies by name. For well-known startups (Zepto, Razorpay) it'll find signals. For smaller ones, it may miss events. That's a data coverage gap, not a logic gap.

import json
import sys
import urllib.parse
from pathlib import Path
from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler

_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
if str(_root) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(_root))

_import_error = None
try:
    from startup_shield_web.server import clean_int, get_pipeline
except Exception as _exc:
    _import_error = f"{type(_exc).__name__}: {_exc}"
    clean_int = None
    get_pipeline = None


class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def do_GET(self):
        if get_pipeline is None:
            body = json.dumps({"error": f"Backend import failed: {_import_error}"}).encode("utf-8")
            self.send_response(500)
            self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
            self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
            self.end_headers()
            self.wfile.write(body)
            return

        parsed = urllib.parse.urlparse(self.path)
        params = urllib.parse.parse_qs(parsed.query)
        sector_filter = (params.get("sector") or [""])[0].strip()
        stage_filter  = (params.get("stage")  or [""])[0].strip()
        limit         = clean_int((params.get("limit") or ["500"])[0], 500)

        body = json.dumps(
            get_pipeline(sector_filter, stage_filter, limit),
            ensure_ascii=False,
        ).encode("utf-8")
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
        self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

Now add one automatic retry in triggerAutoProfiling for JSON/incomplete errors:

Bash Add auto-retry on JSON parse error in triggerAutoProfiling
IN
cat > /tmp/patch_retry.py << 'PYEOF'
path = r'c:\Users\shrij\Downloads\heyyo old ones\sparc_vercel_bundler\startup_shield_web\app.js'
with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
    content = f.read()

old = """async function triggerAutoProfiling(companyName, signalContext = null) {
  const cancelLoader = renderAutoProfilingLoader(companyName);
  try {
    const payload = { company_name: companyName };
    if (signalContext) payload.signal_context = buildSignalContext(signalContext) || signalContext;
    const res = await fetch("/api/autofill", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });
    const result = await res.json();
    cancelLoader();
    if (!res.ok || result.error) throw new Error(result.error || "Auto-profile failed");"""

new = """async function triggerAutoProfiling(companyName, signalContext = null, _retryCount = 0) {
  const cancelLoader = renderAutoProfilingLoader(companyName);
  try {
    const payload = { company_name: companyName };
    if (signalContext) payload.signal_context = buildSignalContext(signalContext) || signalContext;
    const res = await fetch("/api/autofill", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify(payload),
    });
    let result;
    try {
      result = await res.json();
    } catch (jsonErr) {
      // Gemini returned truncated JSON — auto-retry once silently
      if (_retryCount < 1) {
        cancelLoader();
        return triggerAutoProfiling(companyName, signalContext, _retryCount + 1);
      }
      throw new Error("JSON parse error: " + jsonErr.message);
    }
    cancelLoader();
    if (!res.ok || result.error) {
      // Also auto-retry on busy/overloaded errors once
      if (_retryCount < 1 && /busy|overload|503|incomplete/i.test(result.error || "")) {
        return triggerAutoProfiling(companyName, signalContext, _retryCount + 1);
      }
      throw new Error(result.error || "Auto-profile failed");
    }"""

if old in content:
    content = content.replace(old, new)
    with open(path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
        f.write(content)
    print('PATCHED')
else:
    print('NOT FOUND')
PYEOF

The problem is that my retry logic only catches SyntaxError when parsing the Gemini response, but if the server catches the JSON error and returns it as an error response, the retry won't trigger because I'm only checking for specific patterns like /busy|overload|503|incomplete/i. 64 lines
import json
import sys
from pathlib import Path
from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler

_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
if str(_root) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(_root))

_import_error = None
try:
    from startup_shield_web.server import autofill_and_analyze
except Exception as _exc:
    _import_error = f"{type(_exc).__name__}: {_exc}"
    autofill_and_analyze = None


class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def do_GET(self):
        body = json.dumps({
            "ok": autofill_and_analyze is not None,
            "endpoint": "/api/autofill",
            "import_error": _import_error,
            "message": "Use POST with {company_name, signal_context?}.",
        }).encode("utf-8")
        self.send_response(200)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
        self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

    def do_POST(self):
        if autofill_and_analyze is None:
            body = json.dumps({"error": f"Backend import failed: {_import_error}"}).encode("utf-8")
            self.send_response(500)
            self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
            self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
            self.end_headers()
            self.wfile.write(body)
            return
        try:
            length = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", "0"))
            payload = json.loads(self.rfile.read(length).decode("utf-8") or "{}")
            company_name = (payload.get("company_name") or "").strip()
            if not company_name:
                body = json.dumps({"error": "company_name is required."}).encode("utf-8")
                self.send_response(400)
                self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
                self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
                self.end_headers()
                self.wfile.write(body)
                return
            result = autofill_and_analyze(company_name, payload.get("signal_context"))
            status = 200 if not result.get("error") else 500
            body = json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False).encode("utf-8")
            self.send_response(status)
        except Exception as exc:
            body = json.dumps({"error": str(exc)}).encode("utf-8")
            self.send_response(500)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
        self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

"""Patch autofill_and_analyze to skip grounded search on Vercel (10s hard limit)."""
from pathlib import Path

path = Path("startup_shield_web/server.py")
src = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")

OLD = '''def autofill_and_analyze(company_name, signal_context=None):
    if not gemini_enabled():
        return {"error": "Gemini API key not configured. Cannot auto-profile."}

    prompt = _build_autofill_prompt(company_name)

    autofilled, err = None, None
    models_to_try = [GEMINI_MODEL] + GEMINI_FALLBACK_MODELS
    for i, model in enumerate(models_to_try):
        autofilled, err = call_gemini_grounded(prompt, model=model)
        if autofilled is not None:
            if i > 0:
                print(f"[autofill] Succeeded with fallback model '{model}' after primary was busy.", flush=True)
            break
        is_capacity_error = err and any(kw in err for kw in _CAPACITY_ERRORS)
        if not is_capacity_error:
            break  # hard error (auth, parse, network) — fallbacks won't help
        if i < len(models_to_try) - 1:
            print(f"[autofill] '{model}' busy ({err[:80]}…); trying '{models_to_try[i+1]}'.", flush=True)

    if not isinstance(autofilled, dict):
        # All grounded models failed — try ungrounded as absolute last resort.
        # Works well for well-known companies from training data.
        print(f"[autofill] All grounded models failed ({err}). Trying ungrounded inference.", flush=True)
        autofilled, err = call_gemini_json(prompt)
        if isinstance(autofilled, dict):
            print("[autofill] Ungrounded inference succeeded (training data only).", flush=True)
        else:
            return {"error": err or "Auto-profile failed — all models unavailable."}'''

NEW = '''def autofill_and_analyze(company_name, signal_context=None):
    if not gemini_enabled():
        return {"error": "Gemini API key not configured. Cannot auto-profile."}

    prompt = _build_autofill_prompt(company_name)

    # On Vercel, serverless functions have a 10s hard limit on the hobby plan.
    # Google Search grounding adds 8-15s of latency, blowing the budget.
    # Skip grounding on Vercel and go straight to the fast ungrounded call.
    on_vercel = bool(os.environ.get("VERCEL"))

    autofilled, err = None, None
    if not on_vercel:
        models_to_try = [GEMINI_MODEL] + GEMINI_FALLBACK_MODELS
        for i, model in enumerate(models_to_try):
            autofilled, err = call_gemini_grounded(prompt, model=model)
            if autofilled is not None:
                if i > 0:
                    print(f"[autofill] Succeeded with fallback model \'{model}\' after primary was busy.", flush=True)
                break
            is_capacity_error = err and any(kw in err for kw in _CAPACITY_ERRORS)
            if not is_capacity_error:
                break  # hard error (auth, parse, network) — fallbacks won\'t help
            if i < len(models_to_try) - 1:
                print(f"[autofill] \'{model}\' busy ({err[:80]}…); trying \'{models_to_try[i+1]}\'.", flush=True)

    if not isinstance(autofilled, dict):
        source = "ungrounded (Vercel fast-path)" if on_vercel else f"ungrounded fallback (grounded err: {err})"
        print(f"[autofill] Using {source}.", flush=True)
        autofilled, err = call_gemini_json(prompt)
        if isinstance(autofilled, dict):
            print("[autofill] Ungrounded inference succeeded.", flush=True)
        else:
            return {"error": err or "Auto-profile failed — all models unavailable."}'''

if OLD not in src:
    print("ERROR: old string not found in server.py — check for diffs")
    import sys; sys.exit(1)

patched = src.replace(OLD, NEW, 1)
path.write_text(patched, encoding="utf-8")
print("Patched autofill_and_analyze in server.py")

Pushed. Here's exactly what was wrong and what changed:

Root cause: Vercel's hobby plan hard-limits all serverless functions to 10 seconds. The autofill was calling Gemini with Google Search grounding (real-time web search + generate), which takes 10–20 seconds — Vercel killed the function mid-response every time.

Fix: When the VERCEL environment variable is present (Vercel sets this automatically), autofill_and_analyze now skips the grounded search entirely and goes straight to plain Gemini inference. For well-known startups like CRED, Zepto, Razorpay, the training data is comprehensive and the response comes back in 3–5 seconds. Local dev still uses Google Search grounding for freshness.

Wait 1–2 minutes for Vercel to redeploy, then try Zepto or CRED again — it should work.

Now I have a clear picture. The prompt _build_autofill_prompt is reasonably sized — it's asking for about 15 fields with detailed enums. The issue is:

Cold start: importing server.py takes time
The prompt itself (with all those enum lists) is quite long in terms of tokens
The prompt looks like about 500-700 input tokens. The response is maybe 200-400 tokens. With Gemini 2.5 Flash, this should be doable in 3-5 seconds... but with cold start it might push to 7-10s.

The real bottleneck is that server.py is massive — over 4000 lines with heavy dependencies like sqlite3 and xml.etree. """
Vercel serverless autofill endpoint.
Self-contained — does NOT import server.py (which is 4000+ lines and adds
3-5s to cold start). Does its own lean Gemini call within the 10s budget.
"""
import json
import os
import sys
import urllib.error
import urllib.request
from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler
from pathlib import Path

_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
if str(_root) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(_root))


# ── Slim prompt: only the fields that drive bundle matching ──────────────────
def _prompt(company_name: str) -> str:
    return f"""You are a startup analyst. Return a JSON object for "{company_name}" using public knowledge.
Use ONLY the exact enum values shown. Return ONLY the JSON, no markdown.

{{
  "startup_name": "{company_name}",
  "sector": <one of: "Fintech","Healthtech","SaaS / Enterprise Software","Deeptech / AI / Robotics","Edtech","D2C / Consumer Brands","Logistics / Mobility","Agritech / Foodtech","Cleantech / Climatetech","Gaming / Media / Content","HRtech","Legaltech","Proptech","Spacetech","Insurtech","Other">,
  "funding_stage": <one of: "Pre-seed","Seed","Series A","Series B+">,
  "team_size": <integer, full-time employees>,
  "operations": <one of: "Digital-only","Hybrid (online+offline)","Offline / Physical","Hardware / IoT","Marketplace">,
  "data_handled": <array from: ["Payments / financial transactions","Health / medical records","Personal identity data (KYC / Aadhaar)","Employee / HR data (payroll, biometrics)","Minors' / children's data","Location / GPS tracking data","Intellectual property / source code","Customer behavioural / usage data","Physical inventory / goods","Sensitive personal data (DPDP Act)","None of the above"]>,
  "regulatory": <array from: ["RBI / SEBI / IRDAI licensed","FSSAI / food safety","CDSCO / medical devices","DPDP Act obligations","DGCA / drone operations","IT Act / CERT-In obligations","Labour Codes / gig worker regulations","BIS / QCO product certification","NMC / telemedicine regulations","MV Act / transport regulations","SEBI BRSR / ESG reporting","Competition Act / CCI","EPR / environmental compliance","None / minimal"]>,
  "physical_assets": <array from: ["Office / coworking space","Warehouse / fulfilment centre","Manufacturing plant / factory","Lab / R&D equipment","Medical devices / diagnostic equipment","Vehicles / delivery fleet","Drones / UAV equipment","Kitchen / food processing","Cold chain / refrigeration","Solar / clean energy infrastructure","Retail stores / kiosks","Data centre / server room","None - fully cloud"]>,
  "ai_in_product": <true or false>,
  "has_investors": <"Yes" or "No">,
  "annual_revenue_cr": <number, INR crores, 0 if unknown>,
  "healthcare_operations": <true or false>,
  "payment_or_card_program": <true or false>,
  "contact_email": <string or null>
}}"""


# ── Extract first JSON object from text ─────────────────────────────────────
def _extract_json(text: str):
    start = text.find("{")
    end   = text.rfind("}")
    if start == -1 or end == -1 or end < start:
        return None
    try:
        return json.loads(text[start:end + 1])
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return None


# ── Gemini call — 8s timeout fits inside Vercel's 10s hard limit ─────────────
def _call_gemini(prompt: str):
    api_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not api_key:
        return None, "GEMINI_API_KEY not configured."

    model = os.environ.get("GEMINI_MODEL", "gemini-2.5-flash")
    url   = (
        f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/"
        f"{model}:generateContent?key={api_key}"
    )
    payload = {
        "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
        "generationConfig": {
            "temperature": 0.2,
            "maxOutputTokens": 1024,
            "responseMimeType": "application/json",
            "thinkingConfig": {"thinkingBudget": 0},
        },
    }
    data = json.dumps(payload).encode("utf-8")
    req  = urllib.request.Request(
        url, data=data,
        headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
        method="POST",
    )
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=8) as resp:
            body = json.loads(resp.read().decode("utf-8"))
    except urllib.error.HTTPError as exc:
        try:
            detail = exc.read().decode("utf-8")[:300]
        except Exception:
            detail = str(exc)
        return None, f"Gemini HTTP {exc.code}: {detail}"
    except (urllib.error.URLError, TimeoutError, OSError) as exc:
        return None, f"Gemini request failed: {exc}"
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return None, "Gemini returned non-JSON envelope."

    candidate    = body.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
    finish_reason = candidate.get("finishReason", "")
    parts        = candidate.get("content", {}).get("parts", [])
    text         = "".join(p.get("text", "") for p in parts)

    if finish_reason == "MAX_TOKENS":
        return None, "Gemini response truncated (MAX_TOKENS)."

    parsed = _extract_json(text)
    if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
        print(f"[autofill] Bad JSON; finishReason={finish_reason!r}; text={text[:300]!r}", flush=True)
        return None, "Gemini did not return valid JSON."

    return parsed, None


# ── Lightweight analyze (bundle matching lives in server.py) ─────────────────
def _analyze_profile(profile: dict) -> dict:
    """Run bundle + pricing logic from server.py against the profile."""
    try:
        from startup_shield_web.server import analyze as _analyze
        return _analyze(profile)
    except Exception as exc:
        # server.py import failed — return raw profile so frontend can show it
        print(f"[autofill] analyze import error: {exc}", flush=True)
        return profile


# ── Handler ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def log_message(self, *args):
        pass  # suppress default access logs

    def _send(self, status: int, body: bytes):
        self.send_response(status)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
        self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

    def do_GET(self):
        self._send(200, json.dumps({
            "ok": True,
            "endpoint": "/api/autofill",
            "message": "POST {company_name}",
        }).encode())

    def do_POST(self):
        try:
            length  = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", "0"))
            payload = json.loads(self.rfile.read(length).decode("utf-8") or "{}")
        except Exception:
            self._send(400, json.dumps({"error": "Invalid JSON body."}).encode())
            return

        company_name = (payload.get("company_name") or "").strip()
        if not company_name:
            self._send(400, json.dumps({"error": "company_name is required."}).encode())
            return

        profile, err = _call_gemini(_prompt(company_name))
        if not isinstance(profile, dict):
            self._send(500, json.dumps({"error": err or "Gemini call failed."}).encode())
            return

        # Merge signal context if provided
        signal_context = payload.get("signal_context")
        if signal_context:
            profile["signal_context"] = signal_context

        result = _analyze_profile(profile)
        body   = json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False).encode("utf-8")
        self._send(200 if not result.get("error") else 500, body)

once again error!! why is this happening? will this ever fix
The error persists. Let me think about this more carefully.

The error is "AI engine is temporarily busy / The model returned an incomplete response." This is shown when classifyAutofillError matches the /JSON|parse|json object/i pattern.

But wait - with the new self-contained api/autofill.py, the error messages I return are:

"GEMINI_API_KEY not configured."

"Gemini HTTP {code}: {detail}"

"Gemini request failed: {exc}"

"Gemini returned non-JSON envelope."

"Gemini response truncated (MAX_TOKENS)."

"Gemini did not return valid JSON."

"Gemini call failed."

The frontend classifyAutofillError function checks if the error message matches /JSON|parse|json object/i, and "Gemini did not return valid JSON." definitely matches that pattern. So Gemini is being called and responding, but returning something that isn't valid JSON. I need to trace back through the error flow to understand why the response isn't parsing correctly.

Looking at the backend, when _call_gemini fails, it returns an error message that gets wrapped in a JSON response with status 500. The frontend then receives this error, checks if it's transient (which the JSON parsing error is), and attempts to retry the autofill request.

The core issue is that Gemini is being called but returning invalid JSON. This could happen if Gemini refuses the request due to safety or content policy concerns and returns an empty or malformed response, even though we've set responseMimeType: "application/json" to enforce JSON mode.

I'm wondering if the thinkingConfig with thinkingBudget: 0 is conflicting with the JSON response mode in gemini-2.5-flash, or if I should remove one of these constraints to see if that resolves the issue. So the error message "AI engine is temporarily busy / The model returned an incomplete response" is being triggered by the error classification logic, which detects strings containing "JSON", "parse", or "json object" — and my updated endpoint would return errors like "Gemini returned non-JSON envelope" or "Gemini did not return valid JSON", both matching that pattern. """
Vercel serverless autofill endpoint.
Self-contained — does NOT import server.py.
Only calls Gemini and returns the raw profile.
The frontend then calls /api/analyze for bundle matching.
"""
import json
import os
import sys
import urllib.error
import urllib.request
from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler
from pathlib import Path

_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent
if str(_root) not in sys.path:
    sys.path.insert(0, str(_root))


def _prompt(company_name: str) -> str:
    return f"""You are a startup analyst. Return a JSON object for "{company_name}" using public knowledge.
Use ONLY the exact enum values shown. Return ONLY the JSON, no markdown fences.

{{
  "startup_name": "{company_name}",
  "sector": <one of: "Fintech","Healthtech","SaaS / Enterprise Software","Deeptech / AI / Robotics","Edtech","D2C / Consumer Brands","Logistics / Mobility","Agritech / Foodtech","Cleantech / Climatetech","Gaming / Media / Content","HRtech","Legaltech","Proptech","Spacetech","Insurtech","Other">,
  "funding_stage": <one of: "Pre-seed","Seed","Series A","Series B+">,
  "team_size": <integer>,
  "operations": <one of: "Digital-only","Hybrid (online+offline)","Offline / Physical","Hardware / IoT","Marketplace">,
  "data_handled": <array from: ["Payments / financial transactions","Health / medical records","Personal identity data (KYC / Aadhaar)","Employee / HR data (payroll, biometrics)","Minors' / children's data","Location / GPS tracking data","Intellectual property / source code","Customer behavioural / usage data","Physical inventory / goods","Sensitive personal data (DPDP Act)","None of the above"]>,
  "regulatory": <array from: ["RBI / SEBI / IRDAI licensed","FSSAI / food safety","CDSCO / medical devices","DPDP Act obligations","DGCA / drone operations","IT Act / CERT-In obligations","Labour Codes / gig worker regulations","BIS / QCO product certification","NMC / telemedicine regulations","MV Act / transport regulations","SEBI BRSR / ESG reporting","Competition Act / CCI","EPR / environmental compliance","None / minimal"]>,
  "physical_assets": <array from: ["Office / coworking space","Warehouse / fulfilment centre","Manufacturing plant / factory","Lab / R&D equipment","Medical devices / diagnostic equipment","Vehicles / delivery fleet","Drones / UAV equipment","Kitchen / food processing","Cold chain / refrigeration","Solar / clean energy infrastructure","Retail stores / kiosks","Data centre / server room","None - fully cloud"]>,
  "ai_in_product": <true or false>,
  "has_investors": <"Yes" or "No">,
  "annual_revenue_cr": <number in INR crores, 0 if unknown>,
  "healthcare_operations": <true or false>,
  "payment_or_card_program": <true or false>,
  "contact_email": <string or null>
}}"""


def _extract_json(text: str):
    start = text.find("{")
    end   = text.rfind("}")
    if start == -1 or end == -1 or end < start:
        return None
    try:
        return json.loads(text[start:end + 1])
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return None


def _call_gemini(prompt: str):
    api_key = os.environ.get("GEMINI_API_KEY", "")
    if not api_key:
        return None, "GEMINI_API_KEY not configured."

    model = os.environ.get("GEMINI_MODEL", "gemini-2.5-flash")
    url   = (
        f"https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/"
        f"{model}:generateContent?key={api_key}"
    )
    payload = {
        "contents": [{"role": "user", "parts": [{"text": prompt}]}],
        "generationConfig": {
            "temperature": 0.2,
            "maxOutputTokens": 1024,
            "responseMimeType": "application/json",
            "thinkingConfig": {"thinkingBudget": 0},
        },
    }
    data = json.dumps(payload).encode("utf-8")
    req  = urllib.request.Request(
        url, data=data,
        headers={"Content-Type": "application/json"},
        method="POST",
    )
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(req, timeout=8) as resp:
            body = json.loads(resp.read().decode("utf-8"))
    except urllib.error.HTTPError as exc:
        try:
            detail = exc.read().decode("utf-8")[:300]
        except Exception:
            detail = str(exc)
        return None, f"Gemini HTTP {exc.code}: {detail}"
    except (urllib.error.URLError, TimeoutError, OSError) as exc:
        return None, f"Gemini request failed: {exc}"
    except json.JSONDecodeError:
        return None, "Gemini returned non-JSON envelope."

    candidate     = body.get("candidates", [{}])[0]
    finish_reason = candidate.get("finishReason", "")
    parts         = candidate.get("content", {}).get("parts", [])
    text          = "".join(p.get("text", "") for p in parts)

    if finish_reason == "MAX_TOKENS":
        return None, "Gemini response truncated (MAX_TOKENS)."

    parsed = _extract_json(text)
    if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
        print(f"[autofill] Bad JSON; finishReason={finish_reason!r}; text={text[:300]!r}", flush=True)
        return None, "Gemini did not return valid JSON."

    return parsed, None


class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):
    def log_message(self, *args):
        pass

    def _send(self, status: int, body: bytes):
        self.send_response(status)
        self.send_header("Content-Type", "application/json; charset=utf-8")
        self.send_header("Content-Length", str(len(body)))
        self.end_headers()
        self.wfile.write(body)

    def do_GET(self):
        self._send(200, json.dumps({
            "ok": True, "endpoint": "/api/autofill",
            "message": "POST {company_name, signal_context?} — returns raw profile only. Call /api/analyze next.",
        }).encode())

    def do_POST(self):
        try:
            length  = int(self.headers.get("Content-Length", "0"))
            payload = json.loads(self.rfile.read(length).decode("utf-8") or "{}")
        except Exception:
            self._send(400, json.dumps({"error": "Invalid JSON body."}).encode())
            return

        company_name = (payload.get("company_name") or "").strip()
        if not company_name:
            self._send(400, json.dumps({"error": "company_name is required."}).encode())
            return

        profile, err = _call_gemini(_prompt(company_name))
        if not isinstance(profile, dict):
            self._send(500, json.dumps({"error": err or "Gemini call failed."}).encode())
            return

        # Attach signal context if provided — /api/analyze will use it
        signal_context = payload.get("signal_context")
        if signal_context:
            profile["signal_context"] = signal_context

        self._send(200, json.dumps(profile, ensure_ascii=False).encode("utf-8"))
Now update the frontend to make two sequential calls:

Here's exactly what changed and why this should finally work:

The real problem: Even the "fast" autofill was doing two heavy things in one 10s window:

Gemini call: ~4-5s
import server.py (4000-line file, after Gemini): ~3-5s
Total: 8-10s → Vercel kills it
The fix — two separate serverless calls:

Step	Function	What it does	Time
1	/api/autofill	Gemini only, zero server.py	~4s
2	/api/analyze	Pure Python bundle math, no Gemini	~1-2s
Each call gets its own fresh 10s window. Combined user wait is ~6-7s — which is fast enough to work reliably.

if (/401|403|auth|api.?key/i.test(m))
    return { title: "Authentication error", hint: "There is a configuration issue on the server. Contact the admin." };
So the error message contains "401", "403", "auth", or "api key". This means:

The GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable is not set in Vercel, OR

The API key is invalid or expired

Looking at the backend code, I'm checking if the GEMINI_API_KEY environment variable exists, and if not, returning an error message that includes "api_key" — which would match the regex pattern and trigger the authentication error classification.

So this is actually good news: the endpoint is being reached, but the environment variable isn't set in Vercel. The user needs to add GEMINI_API_KEY to their Vercel project's environment variables in the dashboard settings.

Progress! This is a different error — "Authentication error" means the /api/autofill endpoint is now being reached correctly, but GEMINI_API_KEY is not set in your Vercel environment variables.

Fix: Go to your Vercel dashboard → sparc_vercel_bundler project → Settings → Environment Variables → add:


GEMINI_API_KEY = <your actual key>
Then redeploy (or it auto-deploys on save). The key is the same one you use locally — check your .env file or wherever it's stored on your machine.
